Francisco Leung< /name>
<Date>1509177582105< /Date>< Rate>
5<//Rate>
< Text>
We primarily come for the playground area for my kids. There is a decent sized sandbox to play in that will fit many kids. There are 2 main playgrounds for different age levels that are separated by fences which is really nice. Typical swing sets that are on all playgrounds.

The really cool part is that the playground is next to a school that has several basketball hoops and lots of open space for play with lines pre-drawn on the pavement. When school is over, the school's marked pavement is like an extension of the playground for other games.< /Text>

< Text>
Our experience with getting our new cc protection dog has been a journey well worth the while. We were looking for a great protection dog and spent several conversations with both Perry and Brent exploring and identifying our needs. They were patient in allowing me to ask all of my questions. I even flew up to meet a female that we were interested in. Brent and Robin were gracious hosts. However, after meeting us and further discussing our needs they made a recommendation for another dog that was an estate protection dog. We went back and forth and they addressed all our cocerns and shared videos of the dogs.
In the end we compromised and got both! We just took delivery of the first one a week ago. Delivery was a great experience. Tyler, the decoy, was great. He did several real world scenarios with Brent talking me through it all. Your first experience is pretty overwhelming with the bite work. There is no doubt these dogs will protect when provoked!
I will say that this last week has been a lifestyle change. These are working dogs and you have to "stick to the recipe." We work daily with our new dog. You have to be committed to learning your dog and getting him to perform and keep up all the skills he's learned. Brent and Robin have been very response to questions we've had or for feedback on training issues. They are there to support the customers and through the process become friends. We are looking forward to the arrival of our second dog in a few months!< /Text>
